#Lazio
TDA_update_state_2_names = {
	#Roma
	if = {
		limit = { any_country = { controls_province = 9904 TAG_using_italian_names = yes } }
		set_province_name = { id = 9904 name = VICTORY_POINTS_9904_0 }
	}
	#Rome
	else = {
		reset_province_name = 9904
	}
	#Aeroporto Leonardo da Vinci
	if = {
		limit = { any_country = { controls_province = 14123 TAG_using_italian_names = yes } }
		set_province_name = { id = 14123 name = VICTORY_POINTS_14123_0 }
	}
	#Leonardo da Vinci Airport
	else = {
		reset_province_name = 14123
	}
}

	34 = {
		#Wallonie
		if = {
			limit = { CONTROLLER = { OR = { TAG_using_belgian_names = yes TAG_using_french_names = yes } } }
			set_state_name = STATE_34_0
		}
		#Wallonië
		else_if = {
			limit = { CONTROLLER = { TAG_using_dutch_names = yes } }
			set_state_name = STATE_34_1
		}
		#Wallonien
		else_if = {
			limit = { CONTROLLER = { TAG_using_german_names = yes } }
			set_state_name = STATE_34_2
		}
		else = {
			reset_state_name = yes
		}
	}
	#Bergen
	if = {
		limit = { any_country = { controls_province = 9536 TAG_using_dutch_names = yes } }
		set_province_name = { id = 9536 name = VICTORY_POINTS_9536_0 }
	}
	#Mons
	else = {
		reset_province_name = 9536
	}
	#Bastenaken
	if = {
		limit = { any_country = { controls_province = 11407 TAG_using_dutch_names = yes } }
		set_province_name = { id = 11407 name = VICTORY_POINTS_11407_0 }
	}
	#Bastogne
	else = {
		reset_province_name = 11407
	}
	#Luik
	if = {
		limit = { any_country = { controls_province = 14064 TAG_using_dutch_names = yes } }
		set_province_name = { id = 14064 name = VICTORY_POINTS_14064_0 }
	}
	#Lüttich
	else_if = {
		limit = { any_country = { controls_province = 14064 TAG_using_german_names = yes } }
		set_province_name = { id = 14064 name = VICTORY_POINTS_14064_1 }
	}
	#Liège
	else = {
		reset_province_name = 14064
	}
}

TDA_toggle_change_city_names = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_global_flag = TDA_city_name_changes_active_flag }		
		clr_global_flag = TDA_city_name_changes_active_flag
	}
	else = {
		set_global_flag = TDA_city_name_changes_active_flag
	}		
	TDA_change_all_city_names = yes
}
